# 3 Muskeeters approach

Makefile with targets executes different actions. Each of the stages relies on Docker and Compose to be executed. This shows that the application runs the same way whether its local or CICD[any platform]. The AWS credentials environment variables are not set in the .env file but will be passed to the container if they are set on the host using the .envfile parameter in the compose yaml.

$ make create_bucket BUCKET_NAME=c05-3m01-bucket

```
BUCKET_NAME=c05-3m01-bucket docker-compose run --rm c05-3m01 make _test_create_bucket
```
